\\\\textit{nesterov}                                       \\\\\\\\\\n177:             &\\\\hspace{15mm} g_t \\\\leftarrow g_{t} + \\\\mu \\\\textbf{b}_t                               \\\\\\\\\\n178:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                   \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n179:             &\\\\hspace{15mm} g_t  \\\\leftarrow  \\\\textbf{b}_t &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n182:             &\\\\bf{return} \\\\:  \\\\theta_t                                                     \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n183:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n184:        \\\\end{aligned}\\n185: \\n186:     Nesterov momentum is based on the formula from\\n187:     `On the importance of initialization and momentum in deep learning`__.\\n188:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n189:     + rf\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n190:     Args:\\n191:         {_params_doc}\\n192:         lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3)\\n193:         momentum (float, optional): momentum factor (default: 0)\\n194:         dampening (float, This is in contrast to some other\\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\\n244:         by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\\n245: \\n246:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n247: )\\n248: \\n249: \\n250: def sgd(\\n251:     params: list[Tensor],\\n252:     d_p_list: list[Tensor],\\n253:     momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\\n254:     # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\\n255:     # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\\n256:     has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\\n257:     foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\\n258:     fused: Optional[bool] = None,\\n259:     grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n260:     found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n261:     *,\\n262:     weight_decay: float,\\n263:     momentum: float,\\n264:     lr: float,\\n265:     dampening: float,\\n266:     nesterov: bool,\\n267:     maximize: bool,\\n268: ):\\n269:     r\\\"\\\"\\\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\\n270: \\n271:     See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\\n272:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n273:     # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused.   \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n183:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n184:        \\\\end{aligned}\\n185: \\n186:     Nesterov momentum is based on the formula from\\n187:     `On the importance of initialization and momentum in deep learning`__.\\n188:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n189:     + rf\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n190:     Args:\\n191:         {_params_doc}\\n192:         lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3)\\n193:         momentum (float, optional): momentum factor (default: 0)\\n194:         dampening (float, This is in contrast to some other\\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\\n244:         by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\\n245: \\n246:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n247: )\\n248: \\n249: \\n250: def sgd(\\n251:     params: list[Tensor],\\n252:     d_p_list: list[Tensor],\\n253:     momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\\n254:     # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\\n255:     # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\\n256:     has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\\n257:     foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\\n258:     fused: Optional[bool] = None,\\n259:     grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n260:     found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n261:     *,\\n262:     weight_decay: float,\\n263:     momentum: float,\\n264:     lr: float,\\n265:     dampening: float,\\n266:     nesterov: bool,\\n267:     maximize: bool,\\n268: ):\\n269:     r\\\"\\\"\\\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\\n270: \\n271:     See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\\n272:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n273:     # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. (default: False)\n198:         {_maximize_doc}\n199:         {_foreach_doc}\n200:         {_differentiable_doc}\n201:         {_fused_doc}\n202:     \"\"\"\n203:     + r\"\"\"\n204: \n205:     Example:\n206:         >>> # xdoctest: +SKIP\n207:         >>> optimizer = torch.optim.SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.1, momentum=0.9)\n208:         >>> optimizer.zero_grad()\n209:         >>> loss_fn(model(input), target).backward()\n210:         >>> optimizer.step()\n211: \n212:     __ http://www.cs.toronto.edu/%7Ehinton/absps/momentum.pdf\n213: \n214:     .. note::\n215:         The implementation of SGD with Momentum/Nesterov subtly differs from\n216:         Sutskever et al. and implementations in some other frameworks.\n217: \n218:         Considering the specific case of Momentum, the update can be written as\n219: \n220:         .. math::\n221:             \\begin{aligned}\n222:                 v_{t+1} & = \\mu * v_{t} + g_{t+1}, \\\\\n223:                 p_{t+1} & = p_{t} - \\text{lr} * v_{t+1},\n224:             \\end{aligned}\n225: \n226:         where :math:`p`, :math:`g`, :math:`v` and :math:`\\mu` denote the\n227:         parameters, gradient, velocity, and momentum respectively.\n228: \n229:         This is in contrast to Sutskever et al. and\n230:         other frameworks which employ an update of the form\n231: \n232:         .. math::\n233:             \\begin{aligned}\n234:                 v_{t+1} & = \\mu * v_{t} + \\text{lr} * g_{t+1}, \\\\\n235:                 p_{t+1} & = p_{t} - v_{t+1}.\n236:             \\end{aligned}\n237: \n238:         The Nesterov version is analogously modified.\n239: \n240:         Moreover, the initial value of the momentum buffer is set to the\n241:         gradient value at the first step. This is in contrast to some other\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\n244:         by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\n245: \n246:     \"\"\"\n247: )\n248: \n249: \n250: def sgd(\n251:     params: list[Tensor],\n252:     d_p_list: list[Tensor],\n253:     momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\n254:     # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\n255:     # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\n256:     has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\n257:     foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\n258:     fused: Optional[bool] = None,\n259:     grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n260:     found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n261:     *,\n262:     weight_decay: float,\n263:     momentum: float,\n264:     lr: float,\n265:     dampening: float,\n266:     nesterov: bool,\n267:     maximize: bool,\n268: ):\n269:     r\"\"\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\n270: \n271:     See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\n272:     \"\"\"\n273:     # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01KEeqhb9mf3EqJ4fK4qz1AE","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01BhbzWxgSrdAnwCL7aDZq1X","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py","content":"# mypy: allow-untyped-defs\nr\"\"\"Shared utilities for foreach optimizer implementations.\"\"\"\n\nfrom typing import cast, Optional\n\nimport torch\nfrom torch import Tensor\n\nfrom .optimizer import Optimizer, _to_scalar\n\n\ndef _handle_differentiable_and_grad_scaling(\n    differentiable: bool,\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Validate that foreach operations are compatible with grad scaling.\n\n    Args:\n        differentiable: Whether differentiable mode is enabled.\n        grad_scale: Optional gradient scaling tensor.\n        found_inf: Optional tensor indicating if gradients contain inf.\n\n    Raises:\n        AssertionError: If parameters are incompatible with foreach operations.\n    \"\"\"\n    assert not differentiable, \"_foreach ops don't support autograd\"\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n\ndef _update_state_steps(\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    step_value: float = 1.0,\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Update state steps, with special handling for CPU tensors.\n\n    When state steps are on CPU, it's more efficient to wrap the step value\n    once rather than repeatedly during the foreach iteration.\n\n    Args:\n        state_steps: List of state step tensors to update.\n        step_value: Value to add to each step (default 1.0).\n    \"\"\"\n    if not state_steps:\n        return\n\n    if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and state_steps[0].is_cpu:\n        # For CPU tensors, wrap step_value once\n        torch._foreach_add_(\n            state_steps, torch.tensor(step_value, device=\"cpu\"), alpha=1.0\n        )\n    else:\n        # For non-CPU tensors, pass the scalar directly\n        torch._foreach_add_(state_steps, step_value)\n\n\ndef _handle_weight_decay(\n    device_params: list[Tensor],\n    device_grads: list[Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    *,\n    decoupled: bool = False,\n    maximize: bool = False,\n) -> list[Tensor]:\n    \"\"\"Apply weight decay to gradients or parameters.\n\n    Args:\n        device_params: List of parameters on the same device.\n        device_grads: List of gradients on the same device.\n        weight_decay: Weight decay coefficient.\n        decoupled: If True, apply weight decay directly to parameters (decoupled).\n                   If False, add weight decay to gradients (coupled).\n        maximize: If True, gradients have been negated already.\n\n    Returns:\n        Modified gradients list (may be new list if decoupled=True and weight_decay=0,\n        or if coupled and we need to create new list).\n    \"\"\"\n    if weight_decay == 0:\n        return device_grads\n\n    if decoupled:\n        # AdamW-style: directly decay the parameters\n        torch._foreach_mul_(device_params, 1 - weight_decay)\n        return device_grads\n    else:\n        # Coupled weight decay: add to gradients\n        # Reuse intermediate memory (device_grads) if already allocated for maximize\n        if maximize:\n            torch._foreach_add_(device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay)\n            return device_grads\n        else:\n            #             &\\\\textbf{input}      : \\\\gamma \\\\text{ (lr)}, \\\\: \\\\theta_0 \\\\text{ (params)}, \\\\: f(\\\\theta)\\n160:                 \\\\text{ (objective)}, \\\\: \\\\lambda \\\\text{ \\\\\\\\\\n167:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\\\\\\n168:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\\\leftarrow         &\\\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\\\leftarrow g_t + \\\\lambda  \\\\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\\\\\\n171:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: \\\\mu \\\\neq 0                                               \\\\\\\\\\n172:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: t > 1                                                   \\\\\\\\\\n173:             &\\\\hspace{15mm} \\\\textbf{b}_t \\\\leftarrow \\\\mu \\\\textbf{b}_{t-1} + (1-\\\\tau) g_t           \\\\\\\\\\n174:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                          \\\\\\\\\\n175:             &\\\\hspace{15mm} \\\\textbf{b}_t \\\\leftarrow g_t                                           \\\\\\\\\\n176:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: \\\\textit{nesterov}                                       \\\\\\\\\\n177:             &\\\\hspace{15mm} g_t \\\\leftarrow g_{t} + \\\\mu \\\\textbf{b}_t                               \\\\\\\\\\n178:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                   \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n179:             &\\\\hspace{15mm} g_t  \\\\leftarrow  \\\\textbf{b}_t                                         \\\\\\\\\\n180:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\theta_t \\\\leftarrow \\\\theta_{t-1} - \\\\gamma g_t                    \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n181:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n182:             &\\\\bf{return} \\\\:  \\\\theta_t                                                     \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n183:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n184:        \\\\end{aligned}\\n185: \\n186:     Nesterov momentum is based on the formula from\\n187:     `On the importance of initialization and momentum in deep learning`__.\\n188:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n189:     + rf\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n190:     Args:\\n191:         {_params_doc}\\n192:         lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3)\\n193:         momentum (float, optional): momentum factor (default: 0)\\n194:         dampening (float, momentum. Only applicable\\n197:             when momentum is non-zero. (default: False)\\n198:         {_maximize_doc}\\n199:         {_foreach_doc}\\n200:         {_differentiable_doc}\\n201:         {_fused_doc}\\n202:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n203:     + r\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n204: \\n205:     Example:\\n206:         >>> # xdoctest: +SKIP\\n207:         >>> optimizer = torch.optim.SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.1, momentum=0.9)\\n208:         >>> optimizer.zero_grad()\\n209:         >>> loss_fn(model(input), target).backward()\\n210:         >>> optimizer.step()\\n211: \\n212:     __ http://www.cs.toronto.edu/%7Ehinton/absps/momentum.pdf\\n213: \\n214:     .. note::\\n215:         The implementation of SGD with Momentum/Nesterov subtly differs from\\n216:         Sutskever et al. and implementations in some other frameworks.\\n217: \\n218:         Considering the specific case of Momentum, the update can be written as\\n219: \\n220:         .. math::\\n221:             \\\\begin{aligned}\\n222:                 v_{t+1} & = \\\\mu * v_{t} + g_{t+1}, \\\\\\\\\\n223:                 p_{t+1} & = p_{t} - \\\\text{lr} * v_{t+1},\\n224:             \\\\end{aligned}\\n225: \\n226:         where :math:`p`, :math:`g`, :math:`v` and :math:`\\\\mu` denote the\\n227:         parameters, gradient, velocity, and momentum respectively.\\n228: \\n229:         This is in contrast to Sutskever et al. and\\n230:         other frameworks which employ an update of the form\\n231: \\n232:         .. math::\\n233:             \\\\begin{aligned}\\n234:                 v_{t+1} & = \\\\mu * v_{t} + \\\\text{lr} * g_{t+1}, \\\\\\\\\\n235:                 p_{t+1} & = p_{t} - v_{t+1}.\\n236:             \\\\end{aligned}\\n237: \\n238:         The Nesterov version is analogously modified.\\n239: \\n240:         Moreover, the initial value of the momentum buffer is set to the\\n241:         gradient value at the first step. This is in contrast to some other\\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\\n244:         by dampening. with momentum).\\n155: \\n156:     .. math::\\n157:        \\\\begin{aligned}\\n158:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\\\\\\n159:             &\\\\textbf{input}      : \\\\gamma \\\\text{ (lr)}, \\\\: \\\\theta_0 \\\\text{ (params)}, \\\\: f(\\\\theta)\\n160:                 \\\\text{ (objective)}, \\\\: \\\\lambda \\\\text{ nesterov,}\\\\:\\\\textit{ maximize}                                     \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n163:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\\\\\\n164:             &\\\\textbf{for} \\\\: t=1 \\\\: \\\\textbf{to} \\\\: \\\\ldots \\\\: \\\\textbf{do}                         \\\\\\\\\\n165:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: \\\\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\\\\\\n166:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\\\leftarrow   -\\\\nabla_{\\\\theta} f_t (\\\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\\\\\\n167:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\\\\\\n168:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\\\leftarrow   \\\\nabla_{\\\\theta} f_t (\\\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\\\\\\n169:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: \\\\lambda \\\\neq 0                                           \\\\\\\\\\n170:             &\\\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\\\leftarrow g_t + \\\\lambda  \\\\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\\\\\\n171:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: \\\\mu \\\\neq 0                                               \\\\\\\\\\n172:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: t > 1                                                   \\\\\\\\\\n173:             &\\\\hspace{15mm} \\\\textbf{b}_t \\\\leftarrow \\\\mu \\\\textbf{b}_{t-1} + (1-\\\\tau) g_t           \\\\\\\\\\n174:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                          \\\\\\\\\\n175:             &\\\\hspace{15mm} \\\\textbf{b}_t \\\\leftarrow g_t                                           \\\\\\\\\\n176:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: \\\\textit{nesterov}                                       \\\\\\\\\\n177:             &\\\\hspace{15mm} g_t \\\\leftarrow g_{t} + \\\\mu \\\\textbf{b}_t                               \\\\\\\\\\n178:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                   \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n179:             &\\\\hspace{15mm} g_t  \\\\leftarrow  \\\\textbf{b}_t                                         \\\\\\\\\\n180:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\theta_t \\\\leftarrow \\\\theta_{t-1} - \\\\gamma g_t                    \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n181:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n182:             &\\\\bf{return} \\\\:  \\\\theta_t                                                     \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n183:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n184:        \\\\end{aligned}\\n185: \\n186:     Nesterov momentum is based on the formula from\\n187:     `On the importance of initialization and momentum in deep learning`__.\\n188:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n189:     + rf\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n190:     Args:\\n191:         {_params_doc}\\n192:         lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3)\\n193:         momentum (float, optional): momentum factor (default: 0)\\n194:         dampening (float, optional): dampening for momentum (default: 0)\\n195:         weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\\n196:         nesterov (bool, optional): enables Nesterov momentum. Only applicable\\n197:             when momentum is non-zero. (default: False)\\n198:         {_maximize_doc}\\n199:         {_foreach_doc}\\n200:         {_differentiable_doc}\\n201:         {_fused_doc}\\n202:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n203:     + r\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n204: \\n205:     Example:\\n206:         >>> # xdoctest: +SKIP\\n207:         >>> optimizer = torch.optim.SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.1, momentum=0.9)\\n208:         >>> optimizer.zero_grad()\\n209:         >>> loss_fn(model(input), target).backward()\\n210:         >>> optimizer.step()\\n211: \\n212:     __ http://www.cs.toronto.edu/%7Ehinton/absps/momentum.pdf\\n213: \\n214:     .. note::\\n215:         The implementation of SGD with Momentum/Nesterov subtly differs from\\n216:         Sutskever et al. and implementations in some other frameworks.\\n217: \\n218:         Considering the specific case of Momentum, the update can be written as\\n219: \\n220:         .. math::\\n221:             \\\\begin{aligned}\\n222:                 v_{t+1} & = \\\\mu * v_{t} + g_{t+1}, \\\\\\\\\\n223:                 p_{t+1} & = p_{t} - \\\\text{lr} * v_{t+1},\\n224:             \\\\end{aligned}\\n225: \\n226:         where :math:`p`, :math:`g`, :math:`v` and :math:`\\\\mu` denote the\\n227:         parameters, gradient, velocity, and momentum respectively.\\n228: \\n229:         This is in contrast to Sutskever et al. and\\n230:         other frameworks which employ an update of the form\\n231: \\n232:         .. math::\\n233:             \\\\begin{aligned}\\n234:                 v_{t+1} & = \\\\mu * v_{t} + \\\\text{lr} * g_{t+1}, \\\\\\\\\\n235:                 p_{t+1} & = p_{t} - v_{t+1}.\\n236:             \\\\end{aligned}\\n237: \\n238:         The Nesterov version is analogously modified.\\n239: \\n240:         Moreover, the initial value of the momentum buffer is set to the\\n241:         gradient value at the first step. This is in contrast to some other\\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\\n244:         by dampening. This is in contrast to some other\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\n244:         by dampening. &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{input}      : \\gamma \\text{ (lr)}, \\: \\theta_0 \\text{ (params)}, \\: f(\\theta)\n                \\text{ (objective)}, \\: \\lambda \\text{ (weight decay)},                          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{13mm} \\:\\mu \\text{ (momentum)}, \\:\\tau \\text{ (dampening)},\n            \\:\\textit{ nesterov,}\\:\\textit{ maximize}                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{for} \\: t=1 \\: \\textbf{to} \\: \\ldots \\: \\textbf{do}                         \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   -\\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   \\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\lambda \\neq 0                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\leftarrow g_t + \\lambda  \\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\mu \\neq 0                                               \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\textbf{if} \\: t > 1                                                   \\\\\n            &\\hspace{15mm} \\textbf{b}_t \\leftarrow \\mu \\textbf{b}_{t-1} + (1-\\tau) g_t           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\textbf{else}                                                          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{15mm} \\textbf{b}_t \\leftarrow g_t                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\textit{nesterov}                                       \\\\\n            &\\hspace{15mm} g_t \\leftarrow g_{t} + \\mu \\textbf{b}_t                               \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\textbf{else}                                                   \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\hspace{15mm} g_t  \\leftarrow  \\textbf{b}_t                                         \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_{t-1} - \\gamma g_t                    \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\bf{return} \\:  \\theta_t                                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n       \\end{aligned}\n\n    Nesterov momentum is based on the formula from\n    `On the importance of initialization and momentum in deep learning`__.\n    \"\"\"\n    + rf\"\"\"\n    Args:\n        {_params_doc}\n        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3)\n        momentum (float, optional): momentum factor (default: 0)\n        dampening (float, optional): dampening for momentum (default: 0)\n        weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n        nesterov (bool, optional): enables Nesterov momentum. Only applicable\n            when momentum is non-zero. (default: False)\n        {_maximize_doc}\n        {_foreach_doc}\n        {_differentiable_doc}\n        {_fused_doc}\n    \"\"\"\n    + r\"\"\"\n\n    Example:\n        >>> # xdoctest: +SKIP\n        >>> optimizer = torch.optim.SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.1, momentum=0.9)\n        >>> optimizer.zero_grad()\n        >>> loss_fn(model(input), target).backward()\n        >>> optimizer.step()\n\n    __ http://www.cs.toronto.edu/%7Ehinton/absps/momentum.pdf\n\n    .. note::\n        The implementation of SGD with Momentum/Nesterov subtly differs from\n        Sutskever et al. and implementations in some other frameworks.\n\n        Considering the specific case of Momentum, the update can be written as\n\n        .. math::\n            \\begin{aligned}\n                v_{t+1} & = \\mu * v_{t} + g_{t+1}, \\\\\n                p_{t+1} & = p_{t} - \\text{lr} * v_{t+1},\n            \\end{aligned}\n\n        where :math:`p`, :math:`g`, :math:`v` and :math:`\\mu` denote the\n        parameters, gradient, velocity, and momentum respectively.\n\n        This is in contrast to Sutskever et al. and\n        other frameworks which employ an update of the form\n\n        .. math::\n            \\begin{aligned}\n                v_{t+1} & = \\mu * v_{t} + \\text{lr} * g_{t+1}, \\\\\n                p_{t+1} & = p_{t} - v_{t+1}.\n            \\end{aligned}\n\n        The Nesterov version is analogously modified.\n\n        Moreover, the initial value of the momentum buffer is set to the\n        gradient value at the first step. This is in contrast to some other\n        frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\n        of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\n        by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\n\n    \"\"\"\n)\n\n\ndef sgd(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    d_p_list: list[Tensor],\n    momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\n    # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\n    # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\n    has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\n    foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\n    fused: Optional[bool] = None,\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n    *,\n    weight_decay: float,\n    momentum: float,\n    lr: float,\n    dampening: float,\n    nesterov: bool,\n    maximize: bool,\n):\n    r\"\"\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\n\n    See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. We only want to change\n    # the default when neither have been user-specified. Note that we default to foreach\n    # and pass False to use_fused. This is in contrast to some other\n        frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\n        of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\n        by dampening. \\n273: \\n274: Adam.__doc__ = (\\n275:     r\\\"\\\"\\\"Implements Adam algorithm.\\n276: \\n277:     .. math::\\n278:        \\\\begin{aligned}\\n279:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\\\\\\n280:             &\\\\textbf{input}      : \\\\gamma \\\\text{ (lr)}, \\\\beta_1, \\\\beta_2\\n281:                 \\\\text{ (betas)},\\\\theta_0 \\\\text{ (params)},f(\\\\theta) \\\\text{ (objective)}          \\\\\\\\\\n282:             &\\\\hspace{13mm}      \\\\lambda \\\\text{ (weight decay)},  \\\\: \\\\textit{amsgrad},\\n283:                 \\\\:\\\\textit{maximize},  \\\\: \\\\epsilon \\\\text{ (epsilon)}                              \\\\\\\\\\n284:             &\\\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 \\\\leftarrow 0 \\\\text{ ( first moment)},\\n285:                 v_0\\\\leftarrow 0 \\\\text{ (second moment)},\\\\: v_0^{max}\\\\leftarrow 0          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n286:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\\\\\\n287:             &\\\\textbf{for} \\\\: t=1 \\\\: \\\\textbf{to} \\\\: \\\\ldots \\\\: \\\\textbf{do}                         \\\\\\\\\\n288: \\n289:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: \\\\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\\\\\\n290:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\\\leftarrow   -\\\\nabla_{\\\\theta} f_t (\\\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\\\\\\n291:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\\\\\\n292:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\\\leftarrow   \\\\nabla_{\\\\theta} f_t (\\\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\\\\\\n293:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: \\\\lambda \\\\neq 0                                           \\\\\\\\\\n294:             &\\\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\\\leftarrow g_t + \\\\lambda  \\\\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\\\\\\n295:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}m_t           \\\\leftarrow   \\\\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\\\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\\\\\\n296:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\\\leftarrow   \\\\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\\\\\\n297:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\widehat{m_t} \\\\leftarrow   m_t/\\\\big(1-\\\\beta_1^t \\\\big)                   \\\\\\\\\\n298:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\\\\\\n299:             &\\\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\\\leftarrow \\\\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\\\\\\n300:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\widehat{v_t} \\\\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\\\big(1-\\\\beta_2^t \\\\big)              \\\\\\\\\\n301:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\\\\\\n302:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\widehat{v_t} \\\\leftarrow     \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n306:             &\\\\bf{return} \\\\:  \\\\theta_t                                                     \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n307:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n308:        \\\\end{aligned}\\n309: \\n310:     For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\\n311:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n312:     + rf\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n313:     Args:\\n314:         {_params_doc}\\n315:         lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\\n316:             is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\\n317:             LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\\n318:         betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\\n319:             running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\\n320:         eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\\n321:             numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\\n322:         weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\\n323:         decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\\n324:             equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\\n325:             decay in the momentum nor variance. \\n273: \\n274: Adam.__doc__ = (\\n275:     r\\\"\\\"\\\"Implements Adam algorithm.\\n276: \\n277:     .. math::\\n278:        \\\\begin{aligned}\\n279:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\\\\\\n280:             &\\\\textbf{input}      : \\\\gamma \\\\text{ (lr)}, \\\\beta_1, \\\\beta_2\\n281:                 \\\\text{ (betas)},\\\\theta_0 \\\\text{ (params)},f(\\\\theta) \\\\text{ (objective)}          \\\\\\\\\\n282:             &\\\\hspace{13mm}      \\\\lambda \\\\text{ (weight decay)},  \\\\: \\\\textit{amsgrad},\\n283:                 \\\\:\\\\textit{maximize},  \\\\: \\\\epsilon \\\\text{ (epsilon)}                              \\\\\\\\\\n284:             &\\\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 \\\\leftarrow 0 \\\\text{ ( first moment)},\\n285:                 v_0\\\\leftarrow 0 \\\\text{ (second moment)},\\\\: v_0^{max}\\\\leftarrow 0          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n286:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\\\\\\n287:             &\\\\textbf{for} \\\\: t=1 \\\\: \\\\textbf{to} \\\\: \\\\ldots \\\\: \\\\textbf{do}                         \\\\\\\\\\n288: \\n289:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: \\\\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\\\\\\n290:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\\\leftarrow   -\\\\nabla_{\\\\theta} f_t (\\\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\\\\\\n291:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\\\\\\n292:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\\\leftarrow   \\\\nabla_{\\\\theta} f_t (\\\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\\\\\\n293:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: \\\\lambda \\\\neq 0                                           \\\\\\\\\\n294:             &\\\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\\\leftarrow g_t + \\\\lambda  \\\\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\\\\\\n295:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}m_t           \\\\leftarrow   \\\\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\\\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\\\\\\n296:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\\\leftarrow   \\\\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\\\\\\n297:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\widehat{m_t} \\\\leftarrow   m_t/\\\\big(1-\\\\beta_1^t \\\\big)                   \\\\\\\\\\n298:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\\\\\\n299:             &\\\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\\\leftarrow \\\\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\\\\\\n300:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\widehat{v_t} \\\\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\\\big(1-\\\\beta_2^t \\\\big)              \\\\\\\\\\n301:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\\\\\\n302:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\widehat{v_t} \\\\leftarrow   v_t/\\\\big(1-\\\\beta_2^t \\\\big)                  \\\\\\\\\\n303:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\theta_t \\\\leftarrow \\\\theta_{t-1} - \\\\gamma \\\\widehat{m_t}/\\n304:                 \\\\big(\\\\sqrt{\\\\widehat{v_t}} + \\\\epsilon \\\\big)                                       \\\\\\\\\\n305:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n306:             &\\\\bf{return} \\\\:  \\\\theta_t                                                     \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n307:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n308:        \\\\end{aligned}\\n309: \\n310:     For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\\n311:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n312:     + rf\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n313:     Args:\\n314:         {_params_doc}\\n315:         lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\\n316:             is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\\n317:             LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\\n318:         betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\\n319:             running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\\n320:         eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\\n321:             numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\\n322:         weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\\n323:         decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\\n324:             equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\\n325:             decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\\n326:         amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\\n327:             algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\\n328:             (default: False)\\n329:         {_foreach_doc}\\n330:         {_maximize_doc}\\n331:         {_capturable_doc}\\n332:         {_differentiable_doc}\\n333:         {_fused_doc}\\n334:     .. \\n345: def _single_tensor_adam(\\n346:     params: list[Tensor],\\n347:     grads: list[Tensor],\\n348:     exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\\n349:     exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\\n350:     max_exp_avg_sqs: The alpha is required to assure we go to the right overload.\\n668:         if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and device_state_steps[0].is_cpu:\\n669:             torch._foreach_add_(\\n670:                 device_state_steps, torch.tensor(1.0, device=\\\"cpu\\\"), alpha=1.0\\n671:             )\\n672:         else:\\n673:             torch._foreach_add_(device_state_steps, 1)\\n674: \\n675:         if weight_decay != 0:\\n676:             if decoupled_weight_decay:\\n677:                 #     \\\\\n296:             &\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\n297:             &\\hspace{5mm}\\widehat{m_t} \\leftarrow         &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n302:             &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow   v_t/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)                  \\\\\n303:             &\\hspace{5mm}\\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_{t-1} - \\gamma \\widehat{m_t}/\n304:                 \\big(\\sqrt{\\widehat{v_t}} + \\epsilon \\big)                                       \\\\\n305:             &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n306:             &\\bf{return} \\:  \\theta_t                                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n307:             &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n308:        \\end{aligned}\n309: \n310:     For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\n311:     \"\"\"\n312:     + rf\"\"\"\n313:     Args:\n314:         {_params_doc}\n315:         lr r\"\"\"Implements Adam algorithm.\n\n    .. math::\n       \\begin{aligned}\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{input}      : \\gamma \\text{ (lr)}, \\beta_1, \\beta_2\n                \\text{ (betas)},\\theta_0 \\text{ (params)},f(\\theta) \\text{ (objective)}          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{13mm}      \\lambda \\text{ (weight decay)},  \\: \\textit{amsgrad},\n                \\:\\textit{maximize},  \\: \\epsilon \\text{ (epsilon)}                              \\\\\n            &\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 \\leftarrow 0 \\text{ ( first moment)},\n                v_0\\leftarrow 0 \\text{ (second moment)},\\: v_0^{max}\\leftarrow 0          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{for} \\: t=1 \\: \\textbf{to} \\: \\ldots \\: \\textbf{do}                         \\\\\n\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   -\\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   \\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\lambda \\neq 0                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\leftarrow g_t + \\lambda  \\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}m_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\widehat{m_t} \\leftarrow   m_t/\\big(1-\\beta_1^t \\big)                   \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\leftarrow \\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)              \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow   v_t/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_{t-1} - \\gamma \\widehat{m_t}/\n                \\big(\\sqrt{\\widehat{v_t}} + \\epsilon \\big)                                       \\\\\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\bf{return} \\:  \\theta_t                                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n       \\end{aligned}\n\n    For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\n    \"\"\"\n    + rf\"\"\"\n    Args:\n        {_params_doc}\n        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\n            is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\n            LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\n        betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\n            running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\n        eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\n            numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\n        weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n        decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\n            equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\n            decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\n        amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\n            algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\n            (default: False)\n        {_foreach_doc}\n        {_maximize_doc}\n        {_capturable_doc}\n        {_differentiable_doc}\n        {_fused_doc}\n    .. Note::\n        A prototype implementation of Adam and AdamW for MPS supports `torch.float32` and `torch.float16`.\n    .. _Adam\\: A Method for Stochastic Optimization:\n        https://arxiv.org/abs/1412.6980\n    .. _On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond:\n        https://openreview.net/forum?id=ryQu7f-RZ\n\n    \"\"\"\n)\n\n\ndef _single_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    if torch.jit.is_scripting():\n        # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n\n    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    # Note: ensure type declaration is under conditional check for isinstance\n    # or else torchscript will get cranky about the DeviceDict type.\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDtypeDict] = {(beta1.device, beta1.dtype): beta1}\n    else:\n        beta1_dict = None\n\n    for i, param in enumerate(params):\n        grad = grads[i] if not maximize else -grads[i]\n        exp_avg = exp_avgs[i]\n        exp_avg_sq = exp_avg_sqs[i]\n        step_t = state_steps[i]\n\n        # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n            capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices()\n            assert (\n                param.device.type == step_t.device.type\n                and param.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            ), (\n                f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n            )\n\n        # update step\n        step_t += 1\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # Perform stepweight decay\n                param.mul_(1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n                if differentiable and isinstance(weight_decay, Tensor):\n                    if weight_decay.requires_grad:\n                        grad = grad.addcmul_(param.clone(), weight_decay)\n                    else:\n                        grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n                else:\n                    grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n\n        if torch.is_complex(param):\n            grad = torch.view_as_real(grad)\n            exp_avg = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg)\n            exp_avg_sq = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg_sq)\n            if amsgrad:\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_real(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n            param = torch.view_as_real(param)\n\n        device = param.device\n\n        if beta1_dict is not None:\n            dtype = param.dtype  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n\n            # cast to workaround https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/140601\n            key = (device, dtype)\n            if key not in beta1_dict:\n                beta1_dict[key] = beta1.to(  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n                    device=device, dtype=dtype, non_blocking=True\n                )\n\n            device_beta1: Union[float, Tensor] = beta1_dict[key]\n        else:\n            device_beta1 = beta1\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        exp_avg.lerp_(grad, 1 - device_beta1)\n\n        # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n        if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n            if beta2.requires_grad:\n                # Using lerp to only use 2 operations bc addcmul's value cannot be a tensor\n                # Showing equivalence of differentiable path and nondifferentiable path\n                # expavg * b2 + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                #           add expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) = 0\n                # expavg * b2 + expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg + (grad^2 - expavg) * (1-b2)\n                # expavg.lerp(grad^2, 1-beta2)\n                exp_avg_sq.lerp_(torch.square(grad), weight=1 - beta2)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(\n                    grad, grad, value=cast(float, 1 - beta2)\n                )\n        else:\n            exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(grad, grad, value=1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        if capturable or differentiable:\n            step = step_t\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n                if beta1.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n                if beta2.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n            step_size_neg = step_size.neg()\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2.sqrt()\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                if differentiable:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i].clone()\n                else:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i]\n\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i].copy_(torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sq, exp_avg_sq))\n\n                # Uses the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                # Folds in (admittedly ugly) 1-elem step_size math here to avoid extra param-set-sized read+write\n                # (can't fold it into addcdiv_ below because addcdiv_ requires value is a Number, not a Tensor)\n                denom = (\n                    max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n            else:\n                denom = (\n                    exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n\n            if differentiable:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg.clone(), denom)\n            else:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom)\n        else:\n            step = _get_value(step_t)\n\n            bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2**0.5\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sqs[i], exp_avg_sq, out=max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                denom = (max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n            else:\n                denom = (exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n\n            param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom, value=-step_size)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        # Lastly, switch back to complex view\n        if amsgrad and torch.is_complex(params[i]):\n            max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_complex(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n\ndef _multi_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    if len(params) == 0:\n        return\n\n    if isinstance(lr, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise RuntimeError(\n                \"lr as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if lr.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor lr must be 1-element\")\n\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"beta1 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if beta1.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta1 must be 1-element\")\n\n    if isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"beta2 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if beta2.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta2 must be 1-element\")\n\n    # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            )\n\n\ndef _fused_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,  # self._cuda_graph_capture_health_check()\n\n        loss = None\n        if closure is not None:\n            with torch.enable_grad():\n                loss = closure()\n\n        for group in r\"\"\"Implements Adam algorithm.\n\n    .. math::\n       \\begin{aligned}\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{input}      : \\gamma \\text{ (lr)}, \\beta_1, \\beta_2\n                \\text{ (betas)},\\theta_0 \\text{ (params)},f(\\theta) \\text{ (objective)}          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{13mm}      \\lambda \\text{ (weight decay)},  \\: \\textit{amsgrad},\n                \\:\\textit{maximize},  \\: \\epsilon \\text{ (epsilon)}                              \\\\\n            &\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 \\leftarrow 0 \\text{ ( first moment)},\n                v_0\\leftarrow 0 \\text{ (second moment)},\\: v_0^{max}\\leftarrow 0          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{for} \\: t=1 \\: \\textbf{to} \\: \\ldots \\: \\textbf{do}                         \\\\\n\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   -\\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   \\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\lambda \\neq 0                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\leftarrow g_t + \\lambda  \\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}m_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\widehat{m_t} \\leftarrow   m_t/\\big(1-\\beta_1^t \\big)                   \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\leftarrow \\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)              \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow   v_t/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_{t-1} - \\gamma \\widehat{m_t}/\n                \\big(\\sqrt{\\widehat{v_t}} + \\epsilon \\big)                                       \\\\\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\bf{return} \\:  \\theta_t                                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n       \\end{aligned}\n\n    For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\n    \"\"\"\n    + rf\"\"\"\n    Args:\n        {_params_doc}\n        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\n            is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\n            LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\n        betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\n            running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\n        eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\n            numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\n        weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n        decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\n            equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\n            decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\n        amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\n            algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\n            (default: False)\n        {_foreach_doc}\n        {_maximize_doc}\n        {_capturable_doc}\n        {_differentiable_doc}\n        {_fused_doc}\n    .. Note::\n        A prototype implementation of Adam and AdamW for MPS supports `torch.float32` and `torch.float16`.\n    .. _Adam\\: A Method for Stochastic Optimization:\n        https://arxiv.org/abs/1412.6980\n    .. _On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond:\n        https://openreview.net/forum?id=ryQu7f-RZ\n\n    \"\"\"\n)\n\n\ndef _single_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    if torch.jit.is_scripting():\n        # this assert is due to JIT being dumb and not realizing that the ops below\n        # have overloads to handle both float and Tensor lrs, so we just assert it's\n        # a float since most people using JIT are using floats\n        assert isinstance(lr, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta1, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta2, float)\n    else:\n        lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n        # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n\n    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    # Note: ensure type declaration is under conditional check for isinstance\n    # or else torchscript will get cranky about the DeviceDict type.\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDtypeDict] = {(beta1.device, beta1.dtype): beta1}\n    else:\n        beta1_dict = None\n\n    for i, param in enumerate(params):\n        grad = grads[i] if not maximize else -grads[i]\n        exp_avg = exp_avgs[i]\n        exp_avg_sq = exp_avg_sqs[i]\n        step_t = state_steps[i]\n\n        # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n            capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices()\n            assert (\n                param.device.type == step_t.device.type\n                and param.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            ), (\n                f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n            )\n\n        # update step\n        step_t += 1\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # Perform stepweight decay\n                param.mul_(1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n                if differentiable and isinstance(weight_decay, Tensor):\n                    if weight_decay.requires_grad:\n                        grad = grad.addcmul_(param.clone(), weight_decay)\n                    else:\n                        grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n                else:\n                    grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n\n        if torch.is_complex(param):\n            grad = torch.view_as_real(grad)\n            exp_avg = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg)\n            exp_avg_sq = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg_sq)\n            if amsgrad:\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_real(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n            param = torch.view_as_real(param)\n\n        device = param.device\n\n        if beta1_dict is not None:\n            dtype = param.dtype  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n\n            # cast to workaround https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/140601\n            key = (device, dtype)\n            if key not in beta1_dict:\n                beta1_dict[key] = beta1.to(  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n                    device=device, dtype=dtype, non_blocking=True\n                )\n\n            device_beta1: Union[float, Tensor] = beta1_dict[key]\n        else:\n            device_beta1 = beta1\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        exp_avg.lerp_(grad, 1 - device_beta1)\n\n        # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n        if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n            if beta2.requires_grad:\n                # Using lerp to only use 2 operations bc addcmul's value cannot be a tensor\n                # Showing equivalence of differentiable path and nondifferentiable path\n                # expavg * b2 + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                #           add expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) = 0\n                # expavg * b2 + expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg + (grad^2 - expavg) * (1-b2)\n                # expavg.lerp(grad^2, 1-beta2)\n                exp_avg_sq.lerp_(torch.square(grad), weight=1 - beta2)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(\n                    grad, grad, value=cast(float, 1 - beta2)\n                )\n        else:\n            exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(grad, grad, value=1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        if capturable or differentiable:\n            step = step_t\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n                if beta1.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n                if beta2.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n            step_size_neg = step_size.neg()\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2.sqrt()\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                if differentiable:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i].clone()\n                else:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i]\n\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i].copy_(torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sq, exp_avg_sq))\n\n                # Uses the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                # Folds in (admittedly ugly) 1-elem step_size math here to avoid extra param-set-sized read+write\n                # (can't fold it into addcdiv_ below because addcdiv_ requires value is a Number, not a Tensor)\n                denom = (\n                    max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n            else:\n                denom = (\n                    exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n\n            if differentiable:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg.clone(), denom)\n            else:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom)\n        else:\n            step = _get_value(step_t)\n\n            bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2**0.5\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sqs[i], exp_avg_sq, out=max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                denom = (max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n            else:\n                denom = (exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n\n            param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom, value=-step_size)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        # Lastly, switch back to complex view\n        if amsgrad and torch.is_complex(params[i]):\n            max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_complex(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n\ndef _multi_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    if len(params) == 0:\n        return\n\n    if isinstance(lr, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise RuntimeError(\n                \"lr as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if lr.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor lr must be 1-element\")\n\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"beta1 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if beta1.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta1 must be 1-element\")\n\n    if isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"beta2 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if beta2.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta2 must be 1-element\")\n\n    # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n    if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n        capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices(\n            supports_xla=False\n        )\n        assert all(\n            p.device.type == step.device.type\n            and p.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            for p, step in zip(params, state_steps)\n        ), (\n            f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n        )\n\n    # Use shared validation\n    _handle_differentiable_and_grad_scaling(differentiable, grad_scale, found_inf)\n\n    lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n    # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n\n    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n        [params, grads, exp_avgs, exp_avg_sqs, max_exp_avg_sqs, state_steps]  # type: ignore[list-item]\n    )\n\n    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor and on CUDA, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDict] = (  # &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n199:             &\\\\bf{return} \\\\:  \\\\theta_t
